OBJECT Report 78820 Uitgebrachte offertes Sales PK
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS9.00.SMART.OK;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnPreReport=BEGIN

                  Counter := 0;
                  TellCounter := 0;
                  VerkoperFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER("Salesperson Code");
                  EstimatorFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER(Estimator);
                  ContactNoFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER("Contact No.");

                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                    CREATE(XlApp,FALSE,TRUE);
                    xlBook := XlApp.Workbooks.Add;
                    xlSheet := XlApp.Sheets.Add;
                    XlApp.DisplayAlerts := FALSE;
                    xlSheet.Name := FORMAT('Uitgebrachte_off');
                    xlSheet.Select;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'A1:C1').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range( 'A1' ).Value := 'Uitgebrachte offertes';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'A4' ).Value := 'Status';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'B4' ).Value := 'Status trajectofferte';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'C4' ).Value := 'Traject';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'D4' ).Value := 'Hoofdtraject';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'E4' ).Value := 'Calculatie';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'F4' ).Value := 'Project';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'G4' ).Value := 'Service';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'H4' ).Value := 'Omschrijving';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'I4' ).Value := 'Bestek';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'J4' ).Value := 'Type';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'K4' ).Value := 'Kostenplaats';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'L4' ).Value := 'Offerte';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'M4' ).Value := 'Klant nr.';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'N4' ).Value := 'Klant';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'O4' ).Value := 'A,B,C,D';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'P4' ).Value := 'Eindklant';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'Q4' ).Value := 'A,B,C,D';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'R4' ).Value := 'Offerte datum';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'S4' ).Value := 'Geldig tot';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'T4' ).Value := 'Indiendatum';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'U4' ).Value := 'Geldigheidsdatum';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'V4' ).Value := 'Verwachte orderdatum';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'W4' ).Value := 'Planning geinformeerd';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'X4' ).Value := 'Behandelaar';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'Y4' ).Value := 'Verkoper';
                    xlSheet.Range( 'Z4' ).Value := 'Ingevoerd door';
                    xlSheet.Range('AA4' ).Value := 'Tellend';
                    xlSheet.Range('AB4' ).Value := 'Offertebedrag';
                    xlSheet.Range('AC4' ).Value := 'Kans';
                    xlSheet.Range('AD4' ).Value := 'OH';
                    xlSheet.Range('AE4' ).Value := 'Rol Peek';
                    xlSheet.Range('AF4' ).Value := 'Offer Type';
                    xlSheet.Range('AG4' ).Value := 'Type of Work';
                    xlSheet.Range('AH4').Value := 'Category';
                    xlSheet.Range('AI4').Value := 'Products 1';
                    xlSheet.Range('AJ4').Value := 'Products 1 Amount';
                    xlSheet.Range('AK4').Value := 'Products 2'; ;
                    xlSheet.Range('AL4').Value := 'Products 2 Amount';
                    xlSheet.Range('AM4').Value := '100% offerte';
                    xlSheet.Range('AN4').Value := 'Opmerkingen';

                    xlSheet.Range('A1:AN4').Font.Bold := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('A4:AN4').AutoFilter;
                    xlSheet.Range('A4:AN4').Interior.ColorIndex(36);
                    RowNo := 4;
                  END;
                END;

    OnPostReport=VAR
                   TempRange@1100525000 : Text[30];
                 BEGIN

                   IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                     xlSheet.Cells.Select;
                     xlSheet.Cells.EntireColumn.AutoFit ;
                     xlSheet.Range('A1').Select;

                     XlApp.Visible := TRUE;
                     XlApp.UserControl := TRUE;
                     ERROR('');
                   END;;
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525000;;DataItem;PageLoop          ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1)) }

    { 1100525126;1;Column;Number_PageLoop    ;
               SourceExpr=PageLoop.Number }

    { 1100525114;1;Column;PageLoopGROUP      ;
               SourceExpr='PageLoop' }

    { 1100525006;1;Column;COMPANYNAME_ExtensionContract;
               SourceExpr=COMPANYNAME }

    { 1100525007;1;Column;FORMATTODAY_ExtensionContract;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(CURRENTDATETIME) }

    { 1100525111;1;Column;Counter_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=Counter }

    { 1100525112;1;Column;TellCounter_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=TellCounter }

    { 1100525100;1;Column;SubTotal1SubTotal2PLUSSubTotal3_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=SubTotal[1]+SubTotal[2]+SubTotal[3] }

    { 1100525001;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012758;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Code);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               ReqFilterFields=Estimator,Contact No.,Salesperson Code,Contact No.,Leading }

    { 1100525002;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012750;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Code);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               LastFieldNo := FIELDNO(Code);
                               CheckTryOutQuotes;

                               //IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                               //  FOR ColNo := 1 TO 2 DO BEGIN
                               //    CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                               //  END;
                               //  xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := 'LEADS';
                               //  xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                               //  RowNo += 2;
                               //END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525001 : Record 13;
                                  TryOutQuote@1100525000 : Record 11012758;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER(Leading) <> '' THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF "Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET("Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;
                                  TrajectStatus := COPYSTR(Status,1,3);
                                  NaamEindklant := CheckEindklant(Code);
                                  Change := CheckChance(Code);

                                  CheckFinal('', Code, 0);

                                  IF (Uitgebreid) AND (Status = 'T00  LEAD') THEN BEGIN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                    RowNo += 1;
                                    //R ColNo := 1 TO 31 DO BEGIN //Replace JvL
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 39 DO BEGIN //Replace JvL
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[ 1]).Value := TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[ 3]).Value := Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde [4]).Value := "Try-out"."Main Try-out";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[ 8]).Value := Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Lead';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    IF "Expected Order Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := "Expected Order Date";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value := NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := "Order Amount (LCY)";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value := Change;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[39]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(Code,TRUE));
                                    FormatExcel(0);
                                  END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Code,Salesperson Code,Global Dimension 1 Code }

    { 1100525047;2;Column;TryOutGROUP        ;
               SourceExpr='TryOut' }

    { 1100525005;1;DataItem;Uitgebrachte     ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               IF FilterOpt IN [FilterOpt::Mondeling, FilterOpt::"On hold"] THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               TempUitgebrachteOffertes.RESET;
                               IF VerkoperFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempUitgebrachteOffertes.SETFILTER("Salesperson Code",VerkoperFilter);
                               IF EstimatorFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempUitgebrachteOffertes.SETFILTER(Estimator,EstimatorFilter);
                               IF ContactNoFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempUitgebrachteOffertes.SETFILTER("Contact No.",ContactNoFilter);

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempUitgebrachteOffertes.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525001 : Record 13;
                                  TryOutQuote@1100525000 : Record 11012758;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempUitgebrachteOffertes.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempUitgebrachteOffertes.NEXT;

                                  Counter += 1;

                                  TempUitgebrachteOffertes.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");
                                  Tellend             := FALSE;
                                  TrajectStatus       := COPYSTR(GetTryOutStatus(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No."),1,3);
                                  TrjectOffStatus     := COPYSTR(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Status,1,3);
                                  ExpectedOrderDate   := GetExpectedOrderDateTryOut(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No.");
                                  VerwachtOrderbedrag := GetVerwachtOrderbedrag(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No.");
                                  Tellend             := CheckLeadingOffer(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code);

                                  IF Tellend THEN
                                    TellCounter += 1;

                                  Change          := CheckChanceq(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code);
                                  Onderhoud       := CheckOnderhoud(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code);    //JvL 2010-07-09
                                  NaamEindklant   := CheckEindklant(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No.");    //JvL 2010-07-09
                                  EHD             := CheckEHD(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No."); //JvL 2010-07-09
                                  Ingpepland      := CheckIngepland(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code);    //JvL 2010-07-09
                                  GeldigTotDatum  := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Valid Until";
                                  EstimateStr     := CheckEstimateNo(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code,TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No.");

                                  SubTotal[3]     += VerwachtOrderbedrag; //JvL

                                  CLEAR(Behandelaar);
                                  IF TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Estimator <>'' THEN
                                    Behandelaar   := GetBehandelaar(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Estimator);

                                  IF TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;

                                  CheckFinal(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code, TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No.",1);

                                  //Insert JvL 2010-07-09
                                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN

                                    RowNo += 1;

                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 40 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TrjectOffStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := EHD;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := EstimateStr;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := CheckProjectNo(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No.",TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := CheckServiceNo(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Try-out No.",TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Tender No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Uitgebrachte offerte';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Contact No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Contact Name";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := CheckABCD(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Contact No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    IF TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Send Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Send Date";
                                    IF TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Valid Until" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Valid Until";
                                    IF TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Assign Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Assign Date";
                                    IF TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Tender Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Tender Date";
                                    IF ExpectedOrderDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Value := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := Ingpepland;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[24]).Value := Behandelaar;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[25]).Value := NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value := TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Inserted By";
                                    IF Tellend THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[27]).Value := 'Ja' + ' ' + ShowWarning
                                    ELSE
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[27]).Value := 'Nee';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := VerwachtOrderbedrag;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := Change;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value := Onderhoud;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[31]).Value := CheckRolPeek   (TryOutQuoteCode);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := CheckOfferType (TryOutQuoteCode);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[33]).Value := CheckTypeOfWork(TryOutQuoteCode);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[34]).Value := CheckFeature(TryOutQuoteCode,'Category');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[35]).Value := CheckFeature(TryOutQuoteCode,'Products 1' );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[36]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(TryOutQuoteCode,'Products 1' ));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[37]).Value := CheckFeature(TryOutQuoteCode,'Products 2'    );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[38]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(TryOutQuoteCode,'Products 2' ));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[39]).Value := CheckFeature(TryOutQuoteCode,'100% offerte'    );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[40]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(TryOutQuoteCode,FALSE));
                                    FormatExcel(1);
                                  END;
                                  //End replace - JvL 2010-07-09

                                  //FROM SECTION
                                  ShowUI1 := (NOT Uitgebreid);
                                  ShowUI2 := (NOT Uitgebreid AND (TRUE));
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525104;2;Column;ShowUI1            ;
               SourceExpr=ShowUI1 }

    { 1100525103;2;Column;ShowUI2            ;

    { 1100525110;2;Column;UitgebrachteGROUP  ;

    { 1100525085;2;Column;CheckABCDTempUitgebrachteOffertesContactNo_Uitgebrachte;

    { 1100525086;2;Column;NaamEindklant_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=NaamEindklant }

    { 1100525087;2;Column;CheckABCDNrEindklant_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=CheckABCD(NrEindklant) }

    { 1100525009;2;Column;TempUitgebrachteOffertesSendDate;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Send Date") }

    { 1100525010;2;Column;BoldGeldigTotDatum_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(BoldGeldigTotDatum) }

    { 1100525011;2;Column;TempUitgebrachteOffertesValidUntil_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Valid Until") }

    { 1100525012;2;Column;TempUitgebrachteOffertesRegisterDate_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Register Date") }

    { 1100525013;2;Column;TempUitgebrachteOffertesTenderDate_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Tender Date") }

    { 1100525014;2;Column;BoldVerwOrderDatum_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(BoldVerwOrderDatum) }

    { 1100525015;2;Column;ExpectedOrderDate_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(ExpectedOrderDate) }

    { 1100525016;2;Column;TempUitgebrachteOffertesCreationDate_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=FORMAT(TempUitgebrachteOffertes."Creation Date") }

    { 1100525017;2;Column;Behandelaar_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=Behandelaar }

    { 1100525019;2;Column;NaamVerkoper_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=NaamVerkoper }

    { 1100525020;2;Column;Tellend_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=Tellend }

    { 1100525021;2;Column;ShowWarning_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=ShowWarning }

    { 1100525022;2;Column;VerwachtOrderbedrag_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=VerwachtOrderbedrag }

    { 1100525023;2;Column;Change_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=Change }

    { 1100525024;2;Column;Onderhoud_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=Onderhoud }

    { 1100525025;2;Column;CheckOfferTypeTempUitgebrachteOffertesCode_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=CheckOfferType(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code) }

    { 1100525026;2;Column;CheckTypeOfWorkTempUitgebrachteOffertesCode_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=CheckTypeOfWork(TempUitgebrachteOffertes.Code) }

    { 1100525027;2;Column;SubTotal3_Uitgebrachte;
               SourceExpr=SubTotal[3] }

    { 1100525018;1;DataItem;Mondeling        ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               IF FilterOpt IN [FilterOpt::"On hold", FilterOpt::Uitgebracht] THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               TempAanvragenMondeling.RESET;
                               IF VerkoperFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragenMondeling.SETFILTER("Salesperson Code",VerkoperFilter);
                               IF EstimatorFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragenMondeling.SETFILTER(Estimator,EstimatorFilter);
                               IF ContactNoFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempAanvragenMondeling.SETFILTER("Contact No.",ContactNoFilter);
                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempAanvragenMondeling.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525000 : Record 13;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempAanvragenMondeling.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempAanvragenMondeling.NEXT;

                                  Counter += 1;

                                  Tellend := FALSE;
                                  TempAanvragenMondeling.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");

                                  TrajectStatus       := COPYSTR(GetTryOutStatus(TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No."),1,3);
                                  TrjectOffStatus     := COPYSTR(TempAanvragenMondeling.Status,1,3);
                                  ExpectedOrderDate   := GetExpectedOrderDateTryOut(TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No.");
                                  GeldigTotDatum      := TempAanvragenMondeling."Valid Until";
                                  VerwachtOrderbedrag := GetVerwachtOrderbedrag(TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No.");
                                  Tellend             := CheckLeadingOffer(TempAanvragenMondeling.Code);
                                  Change              := CheckChanceq(TempAanvragenMondeling.Code);
                                  Onderhoud           := CheckOnderhoud(TempAanvragenMondeling.Code);
                                  NaamEindklant       := CheckEindklant(TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No.");
                                  EstimateStr         := CheckEstimateNo(TempAanvragenMondeling.Code,TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No.");

                                  CLEAR(Behandelaar);
                                  IF TempAanvragenMondeling.Estimator <>'' THEN
                                    Behandelaar := GetBehandelaar(TempAanvragenMondeling.Estimator);

                                  IF Tellend THEN
                                    TellCounter += 1;

                                  IF TempAanvragenMondeling."Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET(TempAanvragenMondeling."Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;

                                  SubTotal[1] += VerwachtOrderbedrag; //JvL

                                  CheckFinal(TempAanvragenMondeling.Code, TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No.",2);

                                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN

                                    RowNo += 1;

                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 40 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TrjectOffStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := EHD;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := EstimateStr;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := CheckProjectNo(TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No.",TempAanvragenMondeling.Code);
                                  //  IF MultiProj THEN
                                  //    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Interior.ColorIndex(36);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := CheckServiceNo(TempAanvragenMondeling."Try-out No.",TempAanvragenMondeling.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Tender No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Mondeling';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling.Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Contact No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Contact Name";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := CheckABCD(TempAanvragenMondeling."Contact No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);

                                    IF TempAanvragenMondeling."Send Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Send Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragenMondeling."Valid Until" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Valid Until";
                                    IF TempAanvragenMondeling."Assign Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Assign Date";
                                    IF TempAanvragenMondeling."Tender Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := TempAanvragenMondeling."Tender Date";
                                    IF ExpectedOrderDate <> 0D THEN

    PROCEDURE FillTempAanvragenMondeling@1000000005(TryOutQ@1000000000 : Record 11012758);

      TempAanvragenMondeling.INSERT;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckTryOutQuotes@1000000017();
    VAR
      TryOutQuote@1000000000 : Record 11012758;
    BEGIN
      IF TryOutQuote.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          CASE TryOutQuote.Status OF
            //Mondeling
            'T25  VERBAL ORDER':FillTempAanvragenMondeling(TryOutQuote);
            //OnHold
            'T12  ON HOLD':FillTempAanvragen(TryOutQuote);
            //Uitgebrachte offertes
            'T15  BUDGET SENT':FillTempuitgebrachteoffertes(TryOutQuote);
            'T20  OFFER SENT' :FillTempuitgebrachteoffertes(TryOutQuote);
          END;
        UNTIL TryOutQuote.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetTryOutStatus@1000000043(TryOutCde@1000000001 : Code[20]) : Code[20];
    VAR
      TryOut@1000000000 : Record 11012750;
    BEGIN
      IF TryOut.GET(TryOutCde) THEN
        EXIT(FORMAT(TryOut.Status));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetExpectedOrderDateTryOut@1000000060(TryOutCde@1000000000 : Code[20]) : Date;
    VAR
      TryOut@1000000001 : Record 11012750;
    BEGIN
      IF TryOut.GET(TryOutCde) THEN
        EXIT(TryOut."Expected Order Date");
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckType@1000000144(TryOutQuoteNo@1000000001 : Code[20]) : Code[20];
    VAR
      ContactFeatureType@1000000000 : Record 11012753;
    BEGIN
      ContactFeatureType.SETRANGE("Relation Type",ContactFeatureType."Relation Type"::"Try-out Quote");
      ContactFeatureType.SETRANGE(Code,TryOutQuoteNo);
      ContactFeatureType.SETRANGE("Feature Group",'Offer type');
      IF ContactFeatureType.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        IF ContactFeatureType.Feature <>'' THEN
          EXIT(ContactFeatureType.Feature)
        ELSE
          EXIT('');
      END ELSE
        EXIT('')
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckEindklant@1000000104(TryoutQuoteNo@1000000001 : Code[20]) : Text[50];
    VAR
      TryOutLine@1000000000 : Record 11012755;
    BEGIN
      NrEindklant := '';

      TryOutLine.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",TryoutQuoteNo);
      TryOutLine.SETFILTER("Contact Type",'END CUSTOMER');
      IF TryOutLine.COUNT > 1 THEN BEGIN
        IF TryOutLine.FINDFIRST THEN
          ERROR(Text003,TryOutLine."Try-out No.");
      END;
      IF TryOutLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        TryOutLine.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");
        NrEindklant := TryOutLine."Contact No.";
        EXIT(TryOutLine."Contact Name");
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckProjectNo@1000000142(tryout@1000000001 : Code[20];tryoutquote@1000000002 : Code[20]) ReturnStr : Code[1024];
    VAR
      TryoutSuccessor@1000000000 : Record 11012761;
    BEGIN
      MultiProj := FALSE;
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",tryout);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out Quote",tryoutquote);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Project No.",'<>%1','');
      IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
          MultiProj := TRUE;
        IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          ReturnStr := TryoutSuccessor."Project No.";
          WHILE TryoutSuccessor.NEXT <> 0 DO
            ReturnStr := ReturnStr + ', ' + TryoutSuccessor."Project No.";
        END;
      END ELSE
        EXIT('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckServiceNo@1000000143(tryout@1000000001 : Code[20];tryoutquote@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Code[20];
    VAR
      TryoutSuccessor@1000000000 : Record 11012761;
    BEGIN
      MultiServ := FALSE;
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",tryout);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out Quote",tryoutquote);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Order No.",'<>%1','');
      IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
          MultiServ := TRUE;
        IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
          EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Order No.");
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Service Order No.");
        TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Contract No.",'<>%1','');
        IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
            MultiServ := TRUE;
          IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
            EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Contract No.");
        END ELSE BEGIN
          TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.");
          TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Location No.",'<>%1','');
          IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
              MultiServ := TRUE;
            IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
              EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Location No.");
          END ELSE
            EXIT('');
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckFinal@1000000010(QuoteNo@1000000001 : Code[20];TryOutNo@1000000002 : Code[20];Type@1000000003 : 'Lead,Verwacht,Mondeling,On Hold');
    VAR
      TryOutQuote@1000000000 : Record 11012758;
    BEGIN
      IF Tellend AND (TrajectStatus <> TrjectOffStatus) THEN
        TrajectStatus := TrajectStatus + ' !';

      TryOutQuoteCode := QuoteNo ;
      TryOutCode      := TryOutNo;

      IF NOT Tellend THEN
        ShowWarning := ''
      ELSE BEGIN
        TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", TryOutNo);
        TryOutQuote.SETRANGE( Leading     , TRUE    );
        IF TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1 THEN
          ShowWarning := '!'
        ELSE
          ShowWarning := '';
      END;

      IF Uitgebreid THEN EXIT;
      /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
      //                           HIERONDER ALLEEN LAYOUT ISSUES                                        //
      /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
      BoldTrajectStatus   := '';
      BoldTrjectOffStatus := '';
      BoldGeldigTotDatum  := 0D;
      BoldVerwOrderDatum  := 0D;

      IF GeldigTotDatum < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
        BoldGeldigTotDatum := GeldigTotDatum;
        GeldigTotDatum     := 0D;
      END;

      IF ExpectedOrderDate < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
        BoldVerwOrderDatum:= ExpectedOrderDate;
        ExpectedOrderDate := 0D;
      END;

      CASE Type OF
        Type::Verwacht:  BEGIN
                           IF (TrajectStatus IN ['T00', 'T03', 'T04']) OR
                              (TrajectStatus >=  'T25'               )
                           THEN BEGIN
                             BoldTrajectStatus := TrajectStatus;
                             TrajectStatus     := '';
                           END;
                         END;
        Type::Mondeling: BEGIN
                           IF TrajectStatus <> 'T25' THEN BEGIN
                             BoldTrajectStatus := TrajectStatus;
                             TrajectStatus     := '';
                           END;
                         END;
        Type::"On Hold": BEGIN
                           IF TrajectStatus <> 'T12' THEN BEGIN
                             BoldTrajectStatus := TrajectStatus;
                             TrajectStatus     := '';
                           END;
                         END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FormatExcel@1000000001(Type@1000000001 : 'Lead,Verwacht,Mondeling,On Hold');
    VAR
      TryOutQuote@1000000000 : Record 11012758;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT Uitgebreid THEN EXIT;
      /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
      //                              EXCEL VELDEN OPMAKEN                                               //
      /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

      //xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Font.Bold := TRUE;

      IF GeldigTotDatum < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
      END;

      IF ExpectedOrderDate < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
      END;

      CASE Type OF
        Type::Verwacht:  BEGIN
                           IF (TrajectStatus IN ['T00', 'T03', 'T04']) OR
                              (TrajectStatus >=  'T25'               )
                           THEN BEGIN
                             xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                           END;
                         END;
        Type::Mondeling: BEGIN
                           IF TrajectStatus <> 'T25' THEN BEGIN
                             xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                           END;
                         END;
        Type::"On Hold": BEGIN
                           IF TrajectStatus <> 'T12' THEN BEGIN
                             xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                           END;
                         END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetCommentLines@1000000004(Code@1000000000 : Code[20];Traject@1000000001 : Boolean) : Text[500];
    VAR
      CommentLineRec@1000000002 : Record 97;
      TempText@1000000003 : Text[500];
    BEGIN
      IF Traject THEN
        CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::"Try-out")
      ELSE
        CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::"Try-out Quote");

      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("No.", Code);
      IF CommentLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF TempText = '' THEN
            TempText := CommentLineRec.Comment
          ELSE
            TempText := TempText + ' - ' + CommentLineRec.Comment;
        UNTIL CommentLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EXIT(TempText);
    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
